Ingredients  2 mediumÂ eggs  125ml vegetable oil  250mlÂ semi-skimmed milk  250gÂ golden caster sugar  400gÂ self-raising flourÂ (or same quantity plain flour and 3 tsp baking powder)  1 tsp salt  100gÂ chocolate chipsÂ or dried fruit such as sultanas or dried cherries (optional)  Method  STEP 1  Heat oven to 200C/180C fan/gas 6. Line 2 muffin trays with paper muffin cases. In a large bowl beat 2Â medium eggs lightly with a handheld electric mixer for 1 min.  STEP 2  Add 125ml vegetableÂ oil and 250ml semi-skimmedÂ milk and beat until just combined then add 250g golden casterÂ sugar and whisk until you have a smooth batter.  STEP 3  Sift in 400g self-raisingÂ flour and 1 tspÂ salt (or 400g plain flour and 3 tsp baking powder if using) then mix until just smooth. Be careful not to over-mix the batter as this will make the muffins tough.  STEP 4  Stir in 100gÂ chocolate chips or dried fruit if using.  STEP 5  Fill muffin cases two-thirds full and bake for 20-25 mins, until risen, firm to the touch and a skewer inserted in the middle comes out clean. If the trays will not fit on 1 shelf, swap the shelves around after 15 mins of cooking.  STEP 6  Leave the muffins in the tin to cool for a few mins and transfer to a wire rack to cool completely.
